        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Her gÃ¼n farklÄ± sistemlerden binlerce veri akÄ±yor. Peki siz bu verilerden gerÃ§ekten faydalÄ± bilgi Ã§Ä±karabiliyor musunuz?

YÃ¶netim BiliÅŸim Sistemi (MIS), veriyi okunabilir ve analiz edilebilir hale getirir.

____

Every day, thousands of data streams flow in from different systems. But can you extract useful information from this data?

Management Information Systems (MIS) make data readable and analysable.
The Konzek Smart Data Platform (SDP) takes this process one step further.

It consolidates data from different departments in a single location.

It uses AI for anomaly detection and prediction.

It accelerates your decision-making with customisable reports.

It immediately detects critical situations and sends notifications with the Alarm Engine.

In short, it doesn't just store your data; it highlights what's important to you.
